# Test Report

Time: 2024-03-30 03:18:52.410396

### Base Program

```py
def numSquares(n):
    dp = [float('inf')] * (n + 1)
    dp[0] = 0
    
    for i in range(1, n + 1):
        j = 1
        while j * j <= i:
            dp[i] = min(dp[i], dp[i - j * j] + 1)
            j += 1
            
    return dp[n]
```

### Input

```json
[86]
```

```

</details>

## Test Case 1

### Modified Program

```py
def numSquares(n):
    dp = [float('inf')] * (n + 1)
    dp[0] = 0
    for i in range(1, n + 1):
        j = 1
        while j * j <= i:
            dp[i] = min(dp[i], dp[i - j * j] + 1)
            j += 1
    return dp[n]
```

## Test Case 2

### Modified Program

```py
def numSquares(var_0):
    dp = [float('inf')] * (var_0 + 1)
    dp[0] = 0
    for i in range(1, var_0 + 1):
        j = 1
        while j * j <= i:
            dp[i] = min(dp[i], dp[i - j * j] + 1)
            j += 1
    return dp[var_0]
```

<details>
<summary>parser endpoint: passed ✅</summary>

```
Success
```

## Test Case 3

### Modified Program

```py
def numSquares(n):
    dp = (1 + n) * [float('inf')]
    dp[0] = 0
    for i in range(1, 1 + n):
        j = 1
        while j * j <= i:
            dp[i] = min(dp[i], 1 + dp[i + -(j * j)])
            j += 1
    return dp[n]
```

<summary>parser endpoint: passed ✅</summary>

```

\"iter#0\": \"int\", \"j\": \"*\", \"dp\": \"*\"}}}}",

    "args": "[86]"

Response: Internal Server Error
```

Actual Output: None

</details>

## Test Case 4

### Modified Program

```py
def numSquares(var_1):
    dp = (1 + var_1) * [float('inf')]
    dp[0] = 0
    for i in range(1, 1 + var_1):
        j = 1
        while j * j <= i:
            dp[i] = min(dp[i], 1 + dp[i + -(j * j)])
            j += 1
    return dp[var_1]
```
